# GCC Optimization Pass Registration and Execution Chain

## Your Task

Trace how GCC's optimization passes are registered and executed during compilation. Find all C/C++ source files in `gcc-mirror/gcc` that: 1. Define the pass execution order (`gcc/passes.def` — the master list of all passes). 2. Implement the pass manager that orchestrates pass execution (`gcc/passes.cc`). 3. Define the `opt_pass` base class and pass manager interface (`gcc/pass_manager.h`). 4. Implement a concrete GIMPLE optimization pass — specifically dead code elimination (`gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc`). 5. Define the tree-SSA pass header (`gcc/tree-pass.h`) that declares pass registration macros. Report the repo, file path, and key struct/function name for each file.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Summary

I have traced GCC's optimization pass registration and execution chain using Sourcegraph MCP tools to find the key files and structures. The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete details.

### Key Files Found (in github.com/sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333):

1. **gcc/passes.def** - Master list of all optimization passes defined using declarative macros (INSERT_PASSES_AFTER, NEXT_PASS)

2. **gcc/passes.cc** - Core pass manager implementation with:
   - Base virtual methods: `opt_pass::clone()`, `opt_pass::gate()`, `opt_pass::execute()`
   - Pass execution methods: `pass_manager::execute_early_local_passes()`, `pass_manager::execute_pass_mode_switching()`
   - NEXT_PASS macros to instantiate passes

3. **gcc/pass_manager.h** - Pass manager class defining:
   - `pass_manager` class maintaining the pass tree
   - Five pass lists: `all_lowering_passes`, `all_small_ipa_passes`, `all_regular_ipa_passes`, `all_late_ipa_passes`, `all_passes`

4. **gcc/tree-pass.h** - Pass hierarchy and interface defining:
   - `opt_pass` base class (abstract)
   - `pass_data` struct (metadata)
   - Specialized pass types: `gimple_opt_pass`, `rtl_opt_pass`, `ipa_opt_pass_d`, `simple_ipa_opt_pass`

5. **gcc/tree-ssa-dce.cc** - Concrete DCE pass implementation with:
   - `pass_data_dce` and `pass_data_cd_dce` metadata
   - `pass_dce_base` base class
   - `pass_dce` and `pass_cd_dce` concrete classes
   - `make_pass_dce()` and `make_pass_cd_dce()` factory functions
   - `perform_tree_ssa_dce()` core algorithm

6. **gcc/gen-pass-instances.awk** - AWK script generating `pass-instances.def` from `passes.def` with instance numbering

passes.def → gen-pass-instances.awk
